					5 Divertimentos, K.Anh.229/439b (Mozart, Wolfgang Amadeus)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 divertimenti (25 pieces)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1803
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Divertimentos&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Divertimentos</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_basset_horns&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 basset horns</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="31 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_players&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 players</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_basset_horns%2C_bassoon&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 basset horns, bassoon</a></span>;
